<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 10pt 0pt; text-align: center; color: rgb(0,157,217)"><B>Chevron Announces Second
Quarter 2023 Performance Highlights</B></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; color: #009DD9"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 22.5pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Reported earnings of $6.0 billion; adjusted earnings
of $5.8 billion</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; color: #009DD9"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 22.5pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Record Permian Basin production, 11 percent higher
than the year-ago period </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; color: #009DD9"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 22.5pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Record shareholder distributions of $7.2 billion</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 3pt; color: #009DD9"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 22.5pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">PDC Energy, Inc. acquisition expected to close

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 6pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>About Chevron</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 6pt 0; text-align: justify">Chevron is one of the world&rsquo;s leading integrated
energy companies. We believe affordable, reliable and ever-cleaner energy is essential to enabling human progress. Chevron produces crude
oil and natural gas; manufactures transportation fuels, lubricants, petrochemicals and additives; and develops technologies that enhance
our business and the industry. We aim to grow our traditional oil and gas business, lower the carbon intensity of our operations and grow
new lower carbon businesses in renewable fuels, hydrogen, carbon capture, offsets and other emerging technologies. More information about
Chevron is available at <U>www.chevron.com</U>.</P>

do not represent a comprehensive statement of Chevron&rsquo;s financial results for second quarter 2023. Chevron will issue its comprehensive
second quarter earnings press release on Friday, July 28, 2023 at 3:15 a.m. PT. Chevron&rsquo;s previously announced discussion of second
quarter 2023 earnings with security analysts will take place on Friday, July 28, 2023, at 8:00 a.m. PT. A webcast of the meeting will
be available in a listen-only mode to individual investors, media, and other interested parties on Chevron&rsquo;s website at <U>www.chevron.com</U>
under the &ldquo;Investors&rdquo; section. Prepared remarks for this call, additional financial and operating information and other complementary
materials will be available prior to the call at approximately 3:30 a.m. PT and located under &ldquo;Events and Presentations&rdquo; in
the &ldquo;Investors&rdquo; section on the Chevron website.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 6pt 0 2pt; text-align: justify"><I>As used in this news release, the term &ldquo;Chevron&rdquo;
and such terms as &ldquo;the company,&rdquo; &ldquo;the corporation,&rdquo; &ldquo;our,&rdquo; &ldquo;we,&rdquo; &ldquo;us&rdquo; and
&ldquo;its&rdquo; may refer to Chevron Corporation, one or more of its consolidated subsidiaries, or to all of them taken as a whole.
All of these terms are used for convenience only and are not intended as a precise description of any of the separate companies, each
of which manages its own affairs.</I></P>

Investor Relations page at www.chevron.com and www.chevron.com/investors, LinkedIn: www.linkedin.com/company/chevron, Twitter: @Chevron,

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 15pt 0 2pt; text-align: justify"><B><I>Non-GAAP Financial Measures</I></B><I>
- This news release includes adjusted earnings/(loss), which reflect earnings or losses excluding significant non-operational items including
impairment charges, write-offs, severance costs, gains on asset sales, unusual tax items, effects of pension settlements and curtailments,
foreign currency effects and other special items. We believe it is useful for investors to consider this measure in comparing the underlying
performance of our business across periods. The presentation of this additional information is not meant to be considered in isolation
or as a substitute for net income (loss) as prepared in accordance with U.S. GAAP. A reconciliation to net income (loss) attributable
to Chevron Corporation is shown in Attachment 1. </I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 6pt 0 2pt; text-align: justify"><I>This news release also includes cash flow
from operations excluding working capital. Cash flow from operations excluding working capital is defined as net cash provided by operating
activities less net changes in operating working capital, and represents cash generated by operating activities excluding the timing impacts
of working capital. The company believes this measure is useful to monitor the financial health of the company and its performance over
time. Reconciliations of cash flow from operations excluding working capital is shown in Attachment 1.</I></P>
